create or replace PROCEDURE         "BRF34_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" ( 
REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 
 
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
   V_FROM_DATE dATE :=  ADD_MONTHS (LAST_DAY (REPORT_DATE), -1) + 1;
 -- v_report_from_date   DATE := To_date (report_from_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
 -- v_report_to_date     DATE := To_date (report_to_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
  --v_currency           VARCHAR2(10) := currency; 

BEGIN 



 insert into BRF34_MAPPING_TABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP
FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE where report_date = '30-jun-2023'  AND
PURPOSE_OF_ADVN IN (9001, 9002, 9003, 9004, 9005, 9007, 9009, 9034, 9035, 9036, 9037) AND
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP IN 'AE';
--
INSERT INTO BRF34_MAPPING_TABLE(foracid,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_DATE)
SELECT NUM_OPERATION,NOMINAL_1,REPORT_DATE FROM brf_treasury_placement_id where report_date = '30-jun-2023'  ;
--
INSERT INTO BRF34_MAPPING_TABLE(foracid,ACCT_NAME,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_DATE)
SELECT ACCT_NO,ACCT_NAME,AMT_LC ,REPORT_DATE FROM brf_treasury_master_tb where report_date ='30-jun-2023'  ;
COMMIT;

UPDATE BRF34_MAPPING_TABLE SET REPORT_NAME_1 = 'BRF34', REPORT_LABEL_1 = 'ROW102A',
report_addl_criteria_1 = 'Abu Dhabi Commercial Bank'
WHERE FORACID IN ( SELECT NUM_OPERATION FROM brf_treasury_placement_id  WHERE TITRE = 'PLLOCBKS' AND CONTREPARTIE = 'Abu Dhabi Commercial Bank');
COMMIT;

create or replace PROCEDURE BRF34_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 

BEGIN


delete from BRF34_DETAILTABLE where REPORT_DATE = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;


insert into BRF34_DETAILTABLE
( foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,NRE_FLG,REPORT_NAME_1,REPORT_LABEL_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_DATE)
SELECT  foracid, CUST_ID, ACCT_NAME,NRE_STATUS,REPORT_NAME_1,REPORT_LABEL_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE, REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1 ,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,REPORT_DATE FROM 
BRF34_MAPPING_TABLE where report_date = '30-jun-2023' AND  REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NOT NULL ;

--MERGE INTO BRF34_DETAILTABLE A
--USING ( SELECT ACCT_NUMBER, ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE) B
--ON (A.foracid = B.ACCT_NUMBER)
--WHEN MATCHED THEN
--  UPDATE SET A.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC = B.ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC;
--  COMMIT;

COMMIT;


END;
